offering. Please <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">click
here</font> to read the press release.</font></div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">For full

contains a description of the rights offering and other information) that was

close of business on the record date of September 28, 2010, to purchase their
pro rata portion of approximately 3.8 million Units of Zion&#8217;s securities Unit at
a purchase price of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">$5.00
</font>per Unit.</font></div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">If the
Company receives valid subscriptions for all of the Units available under the
rights offering, then the gross proceeds of the offering will be approximately
$19 million, before offering related expenses which we estimate should not
exceed $150,000. This figure does not include proceeds, if any, from any future
exercises of the Warrants included in the Units.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Warrants, which will be issued together with the shares of Common Stock included
in the Units, will be exercisable for a two year period, beginning on the
closing date following the expiration of the rights offering, at a per share
exercise price of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">$4.00</font>.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
rights offering is planned to continue until <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">November 15, 2010</font> (subject to
Zion&#8217;s right to extend the offering).</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The rights offering will include an
over-subscription privilege</font>, allowing a stockholder who exercises all of
its basic subscription privilege the right to purchase additional Units that
remain unsubscribed at the expiration of the rights offering, subject to the
availability and pro rata allocation of Units among stockholders exercising
their over-subscription right.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
proceeds of the rights offering will be used to further our oil and gas
exploration program and, depending on the amounts raised, implement our plans to
establish a drilling company to acquire control of the rig currently being used
in drilling the Ma'anit-Joseph #3 well, as well as general corporate
purposes.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As soon
as practicably possible, we plan to mail to holders of Zion's common stock (as
of the close of business on September 28, 2010) a copy of the prospectus
supplement, subscription materials and other items necessary for exercising the
rights.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Shareholders
who hold their shares in a bank or broker name will receive the rights offering
material from their bank or broker.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Please

The securities are offered by prospectus only, and only within those States and
other jurisdictions in which the securities may be sold, and this Newsletter is
neither an offer to sell nor a solicitation of any offer to buy in any state or
jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful prior
to the registration or qualification under the securities of any such state or
jurisdiction. The rights offering will be made by means of a prospectus
supplement that was filed on September 29, 2010, (File No.
333-164563).</font></div>

place some FAQs (Frequently Asked Questions) on our website at:</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Thomson
Reuters Correspondent at the Ma'anit-Joseph #3 Wellsite</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On
Monday, September 27, 2010, a Thomson Reuters Correspondent visited the
Ma'anit-Rehoboth #3 wellsite. There is still much interest in oil and gas
exploration in Israel, especially because of the size of some of the recent gas
discoveries. The Correspondent told me that Reuters plan to run an 'in-depth'
article about oil and gas exploration, due to the great interest being shown in
the subject. He was very interested in our operations and I would not be
surprised if he pays us a return visit quite soon.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">...........................................</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><img src="img3.jpg" alt=""></font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Left
to Right: Ilan Sheena (Zion's Managing Director of the Israel Office) and
Richard Rinberg (Zion's CEO) at Israel's Chamber of Commerce, Tel
Aviv.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On
Sunday, September 19, 2010, Zion attended a meeting at Israel's Chamber of
Commerce. The meeting was attended by representatives of all the main oil &amp;
gas companies exploring for hydrocarbons in Israel, both onshore and offshore.
The purpose of the meeting was to create an organization that will represent the
oil and gas industry to the government, the press, or anyone else, as required.
At present, there is no representative trade body for the oil &amp; gas
industry. I see this as another welcome step in the development of Israel's oil
&amp; gas industry.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">...........................................</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Finally,
here is an update regarding our current drilling operations.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On August
26, 2010, we announced that drilling operations had begun on the Ma'anit-Joseph
#3 well, in our Joseph License area, onshore Northern Israel, and that the
drilling operations were expected to last approximately six months.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Following
our suspension of drilling activities for Yom Kippur, spanning the period from
the evening of September 17 through to the end of daylight on September 18, we
resumed drilling a 17-1/2&#8221; hole reaching a total depth of approximately 3,965
feet.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">When
drilling of the 17-1/2&#8221; section was completed, we acquired open-hole well log
data that provides us with useful geologic information about the rock already
penetrated by the drill bit.&#160;&#160;Following the logging operation, the
next length or &#8220;string&#8221; of casing (13-3/8&#8221; in diameter) was run into the hole
and cemented in place.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">After a
string of casing is cemented in place, integrity tests are performed to ensure
the cement bond is adequate for the anticipated well conditions.&#160;&#160;In
addition to these pressure tests, a cement bond log is run that gives a visual
indication of the cement bond integrity between the casing and rock
face.&#160;&#160;The results of these tests run on the Ma&#8217;anit-Joseph #3 well
were &#8216;favorable&#8217; allowing us to proceed with drilling the next hole
section.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">

      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In
addition to conducting periodic well integrity tests, we also conduct frequent
tests of our surface blow-out prevention equipment.&#160;&#160;During the past
two weeks we conducted such tests and confirmed our surface safety equipment to
be in good working order.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><img src="img4.jpg" alt=""></font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">One
of the safety signs at the Ma'anit-Joseph #3 Wellsite</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">So with
the 13-3/8&#8221; casing firmly in place, we began drilling the next section of
hole.&#160;&#160;As of Friday October 1, we are drilling a 12-1/4&#8221; hole at a
depth of approximately 1,453 meters (4,767 feet).&#160;&#160;Drilling this
section of the well is expected to require approximately four
weeks.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">"In
your good pleasure, make Zion prosper..."</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Psalm
51:18</font></div>
